3b2(rgyud): tu bzhugs te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis bangam dpal gzhan nu

4b3(rgyud): bu'i gling gi sems can rnams ni tshe thung ba lo brgya thub pa sha stag te/ 'dzem dpal sems
4b4(rgyud): can gang dag de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa de'i yon tan dang

5a3(rgyud): bris te/ khyim na 'chang gi bar du byed dam/ me tog dang / spos dang / phreng ba dang / byug pa dang /

5b1(rgyud): 'gyur ro// 'jam dpal sems can gang dag tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa shin du rnam par nges pa gzi

5b4(rgyud): 'gyuraro// 'jam dpal de lta bas na rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu dag tshe ring por 'dod pas de bzhin ga

6a2(rgyud): ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yurdzu na su bi ni sh+tsi ta te dze rA dzA ya/ ta thA ga tA ya/ ar+ha te samyak+saM bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM pu
6a3(rgyud): N+ye pu N+ye ma ha pu N+ye/ a pa ri mi te pu N+ye a pa ri mi ta pu N+ye dz+nyA na sam+b+ha ro bi tsi te/ oM sarba saM skA ra ba ri shud+d+ha d+harma te ga
6a4(rgyud): ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma ha na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ 'jam dpal de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad

6b6(rgyud): pa ri mi ta pu N+ye dz+nyA na sam+b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba saM ska ra pa ri shud+d+ha d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa
7a1(rgyud): bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ yang de'i tshe sangs rgyas bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa dgus dgongs pa gcig dang dbyang
7a2(rgyud): gcig gis tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di gsungs so// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ra mi ta a yurdzu na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dzo ra dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/
7a3(rgyud): ar+ha te saM myaka saM bud+d+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM buN+ye buN+ye ma hA pur+b+he/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dz+nyA na saM bA ro pe tsi te/ oM sarba sa ska ra ba ri shud+d+ha d+harma te
7a4(rgyud): ga ga na sa sung+ga te swa b+hA wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ yang de'i tshe sangs rgyas bye ba phrag brgyad cu rtsa bzhes dgongs pa gcig dang dbyangs gcig gis
7a5(rgyud): tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di gsungs so// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yur+dz+dza na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dze ra dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ ar+tha
7a6(rgyud): te sa mya ka saM bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta praN+ye dz+nyA na sam b+ha ro pi tsi te/ oM sarba saM ska ra pa ri shud+d+ha d+harma te ga gan
7a7(rgyud): sa mud ga te sa~M b+ha wa bi shung+ga ma hA na ya pa raM wa re swA hA/ yang de'i tshe sangs rgyas bye ba phrag bdun cu rtsa bdun gyis dgongs pa gcig dang dbyangs gis tshe
7a8(rgyud): dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di gsungs so// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yudz+dza na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dze ra dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/
7b1(rgyud): an te saM myaka saM bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM praN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta praN+ye dz+nyA na sam+b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba saM skar pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga
7b2(rgyud): na sa mud ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ yang de'i tshe sangs rgyas bye ba phrag drug cu rtsa lngas dgongs pa gcig dang dbyangs gcig gis tshe dang
7b3(rgyud): ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di gsungs so// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa mi ta yurdza na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dzo ra dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ arba te samya ka
7b4(rgyud): saM bud+d+ha ya/ au puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dz+nyA na sam+ba ro pa tsi ti/ oM sarba saM skA ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sa mud ga te swa b+ha
7b5(rgyud): wa bi shud d+hi ma~M hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ yang de'i tshe sangs rgyas bye ba phrag lnga cu rtsi lngas dgongs pa gcig dang dbyangs gcig gis che dang ye shes dpag
7b6(rgyud): tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di gsungs so// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yur+d+ha na su bi ni shIt+ta te dze ra dza ya/ ta thA ga ta la/ ar+ha te saM myaka bud+d+ha ya/
7b7(rgyud): tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dz+nyA na sam+b+ha ro pe tsi te/ oM sarba saM ska ri pa ri shud+haM d+harma te ga ga na sa mud ga te swa b+ha
7b8(rgyud): wa shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ yang de'i tshe sangs rgyas bye ba phrag bzhi cu rtsa lngas dgongs pa gcig dang dbyangs gcig gis tshe dang ye shes
8a1(rgyud): dpag tu medo pa'i mdo sde 'di gsungs so// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yurdza na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta
8a2(rgyud): te dzo rA dza ya/ ta tha ga ta ya/ arba te saM myaka saM bud d+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dzA na saM b+he ro pa tsi ti/
8a3(rgyud): oM sarba sa ska ri pa ri shud+d+ha d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ \u0f7fyang de'i tshe sangs rgyas bye ba phrag sum cu rtsa lngas dgongs
8a4(rgyud): pa gcig dang dbyangs gcig gis tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di gsungs so// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yur+d+ha na su bi ni shrIt+ta te
8a5(rgyud): dze ra dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ ar+ha te saM myaka saM bud+d+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dz+nyA na sam+ba ro pa tsi ti/
8a6(rgyud): oM sarba saM skA ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sau mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ yang de'i tshe sangs rgyas bye ba phrag shi rtsa lngas dgongs pa
8a7(rgyud): gcig dang dbyes gcig gis che dang yis dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di gsungs so// oM ne mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi te A yur+dz+dza na su bi ne shrIt+ta/ te dzo rA
8a8(rgyud): dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ arba te saM myaka saM bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dzA saM b+he ba ro pa tsi te/ au
8b1(rgyud): sarba saM skA ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ yang de'i tshe sangs rgyas bye ba phrag gang gi la klu'i bcu'i bye ma snyed
8b2(rgyud): kyis dgongs pa gcig dang dbyangs gcig gis tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di gsungs so// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ra mi ta a yur+d+ha na
8b3(rgyud): su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dzo ra dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ ar+ha te saM myaka saM bud+d+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa mi ta puN+ye dzA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba
8b4(rgyud): saM ska ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+haM ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ gang zhig tshe dang laMs dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di yi ger 'bris 'am/ yi ger
8b5(rgyud): 'brir 'jug gam/ 'chang na tshe zad pa lA tshe lo brgya thub par 'gyur ro// tshe yang rna par phel bar 'gyu ro// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta a yur+dz+dza na su bi ni sh+tsit+tha
8b6(rgyud): te dze ra dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ ar+ha te saM myaka saM bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mai ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dzA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba se ska
8b7(rgyud): ra pa ri shud+d+ha d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA ya na pa ri wa re swA hA/ gang zhig che dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di yi ger 'bri'i/ yi ger 'bru
8b8(rgyud): 'jug na/ de sems can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten du nam du yang skye ba mi 'gyuraro// nam du yang mi khom par skye bar mi 'gyur /

9a2(rgyud): na su bi ni sh+tsi tA te dze ra dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ ar+ha te saM myag saM bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM buN+ye praN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta buN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro pa ts+ya
9a3(rgyud): oM sarba saM ska ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te so b+ha wa bi shud+d+he mahan ya pa re wa ri satwA/ gang la la zhig gis tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di yi ger 'bri'am/
9a4(rgyud): yi ger 'brir 'jug na des chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong 'brir bcug par 'gyur ro// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri me ta A yudz+nyA na su bi ni shrIt+ta twe dze rA dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/
9a5(rgyud): ar+tha te saM myaka saM bud+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM paN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri me puN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba saM ska ra pa ri shud+d+ha d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te sab+hA wa
9a6(rgyud): bi shud+d+ha ma hA na ya pa ri wa ri swAhA/ gang zhig tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di yi ger 'bri 'am/ yi ger 'brir 'jug na/ des chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong byed
9a7(rgyud): du btsug pa dang / rab tu gnas pa byes pa yin no// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pi ri me ta A yadz+nyA na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dzor dzu ya/ ta thAg ta ya/ aHte saM myaka sa bud+d+ha ya/
9a8(rgyud): tad+ya tha/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa re me ta puN+ye a pa re me ta puN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba saM ska ra pa re shud+d+ha d+harma te ga ga nas mung+ga te saM b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa raM wa re saH
9b1(rgyud): gang zhig che ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di yi ger 'bri 'am/ 'brir 'jug na/ des mtshams med pa lnga yongs su byang bar 'gyur ro// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mai ta a
9b2(rgyud): yud+d+hA na su bi ni shIt+ta te dzo dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ aH te sa myaka sa bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye a pi ri mi ta pu N+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba
9b3(rgyud): saM ska ra pa ri shud+d+ha d+harma te ga ga na sa su mung+ga te sau b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na pa ri wa ri swA hA/ gang zhig tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di yi ger 'bri 'am/ yi ger 'brir 'jug na/
9b4(rgyud): de'i sdig pa'i phung po ri rab tsam yang yongs su byang bar 'gyur ro// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta a yurdzu na su bi ne shrIt+ta te dzo rA dza ya/ ta thA ga tA yA/ ar+ha te sa myaka
9b5(rgyud): saM bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a bi ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dzA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba se ska ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA
9b6(rgyud): ni ya pa re wa re swAhA/ gang zhig tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di yi ger 'bri 'am/ yi ger 'brer 'jug na/ de la bdud dang bdud kyi ris kyi lha dang / klu dang / gnod
9b7(rgyud): sbyin dang / srin pos klags btsal kyang klags rnyed par mi 'gyur ro// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a ri mi ta A yur dz+nyA na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dzo ra dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/
9b8(rgyud): arba te saM myaka saM bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM praN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri me ta puN+yai dz+nyA na sam+b+ha ro pa tsatsi te/ oM sarba saM ska ra pa ri shud+d+ha

10a2(rgyud): mdo sde 'di yi ger 'bri 'am/ yi ger 'brir 'dug na/ de 'chi ba'i dus kyis tshe sangs rgyas bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa dgus mngon sum du lung ston par mdzad de/ sangs
10a3(rgyud): rgyas stong gis kyang de la phyag skyong bar 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas sangs rgyas kyi zhing du 'gro bar mdzad par 'gyur te/ 'di la the tshom dang / som gnyis dang /
10a4(rgyud): yid gnyis ma byed cig/ oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yur+d+ha na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dzo ra dzA ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ ar+ha te saM myaka saM bud+d+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/
10a5(rgyud): oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ e pa ri me ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro ba tsi te/ oM sarba se ska re pa ri shud+d+ha d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te so b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri
10a6(rgyud): wa re swA hA/ gang dag tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di yi ger 'bri 'am/ yi ger 'brir 'jug na/ rgyal po chen po'i bzhi de'i phyi bzhin du 'bring zhing bsrung
10a7(rgyud): ba dang / bskyab pa dang / sbu bar byed par 'gyur ro// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yur dz+nyA na su bi ni shrIt+ta te dzo ra dza ya/ ta tha ga tA ya/ ar+ha te saM myaka
10a8(rgyud): saM bud+d+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM pu N+ye bu N+ye ma hA puH/ a pa ri mai ta buN+ye a pa ri mi ta buN+ye d+hA na sa~M b+ha ro br-i tsi te/ oM sarba saM ske re ba ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swab+hA
10b1(rgyud): wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya ba ri wa re swA hA/ gang zhig tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di yi ger 'brir 'am/ yi ger 'brir 'jug na/ de de bzhin gshegs pa
10b2(rgyud): 'od dpag tu med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams bde ba can du skye bar 'gyur ro// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yur dz+nyA na su bi ni sh+tsi t+ta te dze ra dza ya/
10b3(rgyud): ta tha ga ta ya/ ar+ha te saM myaka saM bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM buN+ye praN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa re mi ta praN+ye a pa ra mi ta puN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba saM ska ra pa ri shud+d+hi
10b4(rgyud): d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA ya na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ sa phyogs gang du mdo sde dkon mchog 'di 'bri ba'i sa phyogs de yang mchod rten du 'gyur ro//
10b5(rgyud): byol song gi skye gnas su song ba'i bya dang / ri dgas gang dag gis rna lam du grags par gyur pa de dag thams cad bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu
10b6(rgyud): mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro// oM ni b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ra mi ta A yur dz+nyA na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dzo ra dza ya/ ta tha ga ta ya/ ar+ha te saM myaka saM
10b7(rgyud): bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA pun+d+he/ a pa ri mi te pran+ye a pa ri mi ta bud+d+he dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba saM ska ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na myang+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he/
10b8(rgyud): ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ gang zhig tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di yi ger 'bri 'am/ yi ger 'brir 'jug na/ de bud kyi lus su nam du yang skye
11a1(rgyud): @bar mi 'gyur ro// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a ba ri mi ta A gur dz+nyAn su bi ni shrId+ha te dzer dza ga/ ta thag ta ya ar+ha te sa myag
11a2(rgyud): saM bud+d+ha ya/ tad+ya tha/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA buN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta buN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba saM skA ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he
11a3(rgyud): ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ gang zhig tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di'i phyir ka sha pa ni gcig sbyin na/ des stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi
11a4(rgyud): khams rin po che sna bdun gyis yongs su bkang ste sbyin pa byin par 'gyur ro// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yur dz+nyA na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dzo rA dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/
11a5(rgyud): ar+d+ha te saM myaka saM bud+d+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba saM skA ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga ga na sa
11a6(rgyud): mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swAhA/ gang la zhig chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la mchod pa byed par 'gyur ba des/ dam pa'i chos mtha' dag la mchod pa byas par
11a7(rgyud): 'gyur ro// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mai ta A yur dz+nyA na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dze ra dza ya/ ta thA ga ta ya/ arda te saM myag saM bud+d+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/
11a8(rgyud): a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro pa pa tsi te/ oM sarba saM ska ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ 'di lta ste/
11b1(rgyud): dper na/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par gzigs dang / gtsug tor can dang / thams cad skyob dang / log par dad sel dang / 'khor ba 'jig dang / gser thub dang /
11b2(rgyud): 'od srung dang / shAkya thub pa la sogs pa la rin po che sna bdun gyis mchod pa byas pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po'i tshad ni bgrang bar nus kyi/ tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med
11b3(rgyud): pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po'i tshad ni bgrang bar mi nus so// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a ba ri mi ta A yur dz+nyA na su bi ni sh+tsi d+ha te dzo ra dza ya/ ta tha ga ta ya/ ar+ha te saM myaka
11b4(rgyud): saM bud+d+hA ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro ba tsi te/ oM sarba saM skA ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi
11b5(rgyud): shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri wa re swA hA/ 'di lta ste/ dper na/ rin po che'i phung po ri rab tsam srungs te/ sbyin pa byin pa de'i bsod nams kyi phung po'i tshad ni bgrang bar nus kyi/
11b6(rgyud): tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po'i tshad ni bgrang bar 'ami nus so// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A phur dz+nyA na su bi ni shrIt+tha te dze ra dzA ya/
11b7(rgyud): ta tha ga ta ya/ an te saM myaka sa~M bud+d+ha ya/ dad+ya thA/ oM buN+ye bu kye ma hA pra t+ye/ a pa ri mai ta pra N+ye a pa ri me ta prad+d+he dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro btsi te/ oM sarba si skAr pa ri shud+d+ha
11b8(rgyud): d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa re wa re swA hA/ 'di lta ste/ dper na/ rgya mtsho chen po bzhi chus yongs su gang ba'i thigs pa re re nas bgrang
12a1(rgyud): bar nus kyi/ che dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po'i tshad ni bgrang bar mi nus so// oM na mo
12a2(rgyud): b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yur dz+nyA na su bi ni sh+tsit+ta te dzo ra dza ya/ ta tha ga ta ya/ ar+ha te saM myaka saM bud+d+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye praN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi
12a3(rgyud): ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi te/ oM sarba saM skA re pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya ba ri wa re swA hA/ gang zhig tshe dang ye
12a4(rgyud): shes dpag tu med pa'i mdo sde 'di yi ger 'bri 'am/ yi ger 'jug gam/ bsti stang du byas te/ mchod pa byas par gyur pa des phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi
12a5(rgyud): zhing thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag byas pa dang / mchod pa byas pa yin no// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta A yur dz+nyA na su bi ni
12a6(rgyud): sh+tsi tA te dze raM dza ya/ ta tha ga ta ya/ ar+ha te saM myaka saM bud+d+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta puN+ye dzA na saM b+ha ri pa tsi te/
12a7(rgyud): oM sarba saM kai re pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+hA wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya ba ri wa re swA hA/ sbyin pa'i stobs kyi sangs rgyas yang dag 'phags/ mi yaM seng
12a8(rgyud): ge sbyin pa'i stobs rtogs nas/ snying rje can gyi grong khyer 'jug pa na/ sbyin pa'i stobs kyi sgra ni grags par 'gyur/ tshul khrims stobs kyi sangs rgyas yang
12b1(rgyud): dag 'bags/ mi yaM seng ge tshul khrims stobs rtogs nas/ snying rje can gyi grong khyer 'jug pa na/ rdul khrims stobs kyi sgra ni grags par 'gyur/ bzod pa na
12b2(rgyud): stobs kyi sangs rgyas yang dag 'phags/ me yi seng ge bzod pa'i stobs rtogs nas/ snying rje can gyi grong khyer 'jug pa na/ bzod pa'i stobs kyi sgra ni grag/
12b3(rgyud): bar 'gyur/ brtson 'grus stobs kyi sangs rgyas yang dag 'phags/ mi yi se ge brtson 'grus stobs rtogs nas/ snying rje can gyi grong khyer 'jug pa na/
12b4(rgyud): brtson 'grus stobs kyi sgra ni grags par 'gyur/ bsam gtan stobs kyi sangs rgyas yang dag 'phags/ mi yi seng ge bsam gtan stobs rtogs nas/
12b5(rgyud): snying rje can gyi grong khyer 'jug pa na/ bsam gtan stobs kyi sgra ni grags par 'gyur/ shes rab stobs kyi sangs rgyas yang dag 'phags/ mi yi seng ge shes
12b6(rgyud): rab stobs rtogs nas/ snying rje can gyi grong khyer 'jug pa na/ shes rab stobs kyi sgra ni grags par 'gyur/ oM na mo b+ha ga wa te/ a pa ri mi ta a yur
12b7(rgyud): dz+nyA na su bi ni sh+tsi t+ta te dze rA dzA ya/ ta tha ga ta ya/ a ra ha te saM myag saM bud d+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ au puN+ye puN+ye ma hA puN+ye/ a pa ri mi ta puN+ye a pa ri mi ta
12b8(rgyud): puN+ye dz+nyA na saM b+ha ro pa tsi taM/ oM sarba saM skA ra pa ri shud+d+he d+harma te ga ga na sa mung+ga te swa b+ha wa bi shud+d+he ma hA na ya pa ri wa re sA hA/ bcom ldan 'das
13a1(rgyud): @kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa dang / thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de dag
13a2(rgyud): dang / lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// 'phags/
13a3(rgyud): pa che dang ye shes dpag tu med pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo rdzogs so// 'di la rten nas bdag gzhan skye dgu mtha' dag 'chi ba med pa tshe'i dpal la dbang
13a4(rgyud): thob par gyur cig/ sarba mang+ga laM/ @##// rgya gar skad du/ ar+ya a ba ra ma~M ta A pur dz+nyA na hr-i da ya na ma d+ha ra ni// bod skad du/
13a5(rgyud): 'phags pa che dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i snying po zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di
13a6(rgyud): skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus cig na/ bcom ldan 'das gang gtas bskor ba'i rdzing bu'i 'gram na/ dge slong lnga stong lnga brgyas bskor ba'i dge slong gi dge 'dun
13a7(rgyud): chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa' dge 'dun chen po dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong rnams la bka' stsal nas
13a8(rgyud): dag slong de dag chom ldan 'das kyis mtshan pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis de dag la 'did ces bka 'phrul to// 'drenas nub kyi byags ril ma
13b1(rgyud): bde ba can gyi 'jig rten khams// de na rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bzhugs// de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med// su zhig de yi mtshan brjod na/ de ni deraru skye bar/
13b2(rgyud): 'gyur/ dge slong dge 'dun bcas te mthong // de na bud med yod ma yin mngal na gnas pa'ang yod ma yin// rin chen rnams kyi pad mo las/ rdzu 'phrul
13b3(rgyud): chen pos 'byung bar 'gyur// zas dang gos dang sman rnams dang // chos gos mal cha lhung bzed rnams// sems kyi bsam ma thag tu ni// de dag mod la 'byung bar/
13b4(rgyud): 'gyur// phyogs bcu bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams// bde ba can gyi bsngags pa brjod// de ltar sangs rgyas bsam mi khyab// sangs rgyas chos kyang bsam
13b5(rgyud): mi khyab/ 'phags pa'i dge 'dun bsam mi khyab// bsam mi khyab la dad byas na// rnam par smin pa bsam mi khyab// rnam dag zhing du skye bar 'gyur/
13b6(rgyud): dge slong dag de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas tshe dpag med kyi pho brang ni/ 'khor dang bcas pa zhes bya ba brgyar dpag
13b7(rgyud): tshad khri yod pa zhig yod de/ rgyal rigs su skyes so// dge slong dag de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas tshe dpag
13b8(rgyud): med kyi yab ni/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po bzang po'i mchog ces bya'o// de'i yum ni gzi brjid can zhes bya bar gyur to// de'i btsun mo ni rgyal
14a1(rgyud): rigs bzang skyong ma zhes bya'o// dge slong dag de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med kyi sras ni zla ba'i 'od ces bya
14a2(rgyud): bar gyur to// rim gro ba ni snyen pa dri ma med ces bya'o// dge slong dag de bzhin gshegs pa che dpag med kyi shes rab can gyi mchog tu gyur pa ni/ bzang po
14a3(rgyud): rtogs ces bya'o// rdzu 'phrul dang ldan pa'i mchog dang / brtson 'grus chen po dang ldan pa'i mchog ni bkod pa chen po zhes bya'o// dge slong dag de bzhin gshegs
14a4(rgyud): pa tshe dpag med kyi bdud ni mchod pa'i rgyal po zhes bya'o// lha sbyin gyi ming ni dang ba zhes bya bar gyur to// dge slong dag de bzhin gshegs pa che dpag med kyi
14a5(rgyud): nyan thos 'dus pa rin po ni nyan thos chen po drag khri yod do// dge slong dag sems can thams cad kyis legs par bsams te/ de bzhin gshegs pa
14a6(rgyud): tshe dpag med kyi mtshan legs par bzung la zhag bcur sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa rtse gcig tu sgom zhing / 'jig rten gyi khams bde ba can du bzhugs pa'i
14a7(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med rgyun tu yid la bya'o// dpal 'chi med rnga sgra'i rgyal po zhes bya ba'i bzung 'di yang rtag tu bzlas brjod bya'o// nyin len
14a8(rgyud): gsum mtshan lan mtshan yan lag lngas phyag byas la/ sems can thams cad kyi de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med bsam nas/ zhag bcu 'das
14b1(rgyud): pa'i 'og tu de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med mthong bar 'gyur ro// phyogs bcu na bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad kyang mthong bar
14b2(rgyud): 'gyur ro// dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyang 'jig rten gyi khams bde ba can du yongs su bsngos na/ de 'chi ba'i dus kyi tshe de bzhin gshegs pa che dpag med
14b3(rgyud): mdun na bzhugs pa mthong bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med de'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing du skye bar 'gyur ro// dge slong dag 'chi med rnga sgra'i
14b4(rgyud): rgyal po zhes bya ba'i gzung de gang zhe na/ tad+ya thA/ sha ba le/ a ba le/ sa ma dza le/ nir de she/ nir dza te/ nir ru ga te/ ni ra khu khe/ dz+wa la ba ra che da ni/
14b5(rgyud): su kha ba ti nir te sha/ a mi te a yu garba nir hA te/ a mi te a yur pras da ni/ nir bud d+he/ a ka sha nir de she/ a ka sha nir ku sha le/ a ka sha
14b6(rgyud): nir dir sha ni/ a ka sha a d+hiSh+ThA ne/ su kha ba ti a b+hiSh+ma ne rU pa nir de she/ tsa tra ri d+har+m+ma sA d+ha me tsa tA ri Ar+ya sa t+ya prA sa da ni/ tsa tra ri marga b+ha na pra sA d+ha ni/
14b7(rgyud): bA la bir+ya pra sA d+ha ni/ d+harma ched ni ku sha li/ ku sha le nir de sha/ ku sha la pra tiSh+Tha ne/ bud+d+ha ku sha le/ bi ku le/ bi shud+d+he pra b+hA/ sarba d+harma ka ra ni/
14b8(rgyud): nir dza te/ nir bud+haM/ bi ma la/ bi ra dze/ ra dza se/ ra sa gre/ ra sa gra ba le/ ra sa gra a d+hiSh+NI te/ ku le pra te ku la bi ku le/ d+han to/ su d+han ta
15a1(rgyud): @tsaM te sa pra shan d+hAHte/ su pra tiSh+Thi te/ su le su mu khi/ d+harme tsaH/ ba le tsa ba le/ a nu sha a ba le/ bud d+ha ka sha
15a2(rgyud): gu na/ bud+d+ha a ka sha ni ra gu ni/ a mri ta dun d+hu b+hi sa re swA hA/ dge slong dag dad pa'i rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang la la 'chi med rnga sgra'i rgyal
15a3(rgyud): po zhes bya ba'i gzungs 'di/ ji skad bstan pa de bzhin du kha ton byed pa des/ gos gtsang ma bgos te/ sa phyogs gtsang zhing dri ma med par/ de bzhin gshegs pa
15a4(rgyud): tshe dpag med la me tog dang spos mchod par bya'o// byang chub kyi snying po pad+ma'i gdan dang / byang chub kyi shing drung phun sum tshogs pa yang yid la bya'o// de la yang 'dod pa
15a5(rgyud): bskyed par bya ste/ 'dod pa dang dad pa byas nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med de'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing du skye bar 'gyur ro// dge slong dag de bzhin gshegs
15a6(rgyud): ba che dpag med kyi byang chub kyi shing drung ni/ rin po che'i blo rnam par snang ba zhes bya la/ shing de'i me tog dang 'bras bu phun sum tshogs pa'o// pad ma'i gdan ni
15a7(rgyud): dag cing gsal la bzang zhing bkra ba'i 'od zer can zhes bya ste/ rin po che du mas bskor ba la/ de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag med bzhugs so// g.yas na ni byang chub
15a8(rgyud): sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug go/ g.yon na ni byang chub sems dpa' mthu chen thob pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs grangs med pas bskor to//
15b1(rgyud): dad pa'i rigs kyi bu dang / rigs kyi bu mo gang la la mos pa dang dad pa mang ba der skye bar 'gyur te/ gser gyi sa bzhi chen po la rin po che sna bdun gyi pad ma chen po dag
15b2(rgyud): las brdzus te skye bar 'gyur ro// dge slong dag/ dge slong pha 'am/ dge slong ma 'am/ dge bsnyen nam/ dge bsnyen ma gang la las/ de bzhin gshegs pa tshe
15b3(rgyud): dpag med pa de'i mtshan yang dag par 'dzin pa de la/ me'i 'jigs pa mi 'byung chu'i 'jigs pa mi 'byung / dug gi 'jigs pa mi 'byung / mtshon cha'i 'jigs pa
15b4(rgyud): mi 'byung / gnod sbyin gyi 'jigs pa mi 'byung / srin po'i 'jig pa mi 'byung ste/ sngon gyi las kyi rnam par smin pa ni gang la yang ma togs so// bcom ldan 'das
15b5(rgyud): kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ dge slong de dag dang / byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang / thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de dag dang / lha dang / mi dang /
15b6(rgyud): lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// 'phags pa tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med
15b7(rgyud): pa'i snying po zhes bya ba'i gzungs sa rdzogs so// dge'o// bkris// // rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya a b+hi Sh+Ti ka na ma d+ha ra ni/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa dbang
15b8(rgyud): bskur ba zhes bya ba'i bzungs/ sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na//
16a1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na/ rgyal po rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na/ dge slong brgyad
16a2(rgyud): stong gis dge 'dun chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa' grangs med pa sngon gyi rgyal ba la lhag par byas pa rnams dang / thabs gcig tu bzhugs te/ de nas bcom/
16a3(rgyud): ldan 'das kyis sha ri'i bu la bka' stsal pa/ shA ri'i bu khyod kyis 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i ma dang / byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa dang / bden pa'i
16a4(rgyud): smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams yongs su bzung ba/ byang chub sems dpa' chos 'di dag sgoms shig/ ston cig/ de dag zhes 'di lta ste/ dbang
16a5(rgyud): bskur ba'i bzung kyi chos kyi rnam grangs so// de nas tshe dang ldan pa sha ri'i bus/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das gzungs ni yul
16a6(rgyud): na mi gnas/ phyogs na mi gnas/ bcom ldan 'das gzungs zhes bgyi ba 'di'i tshig gis don gang lags/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das
16a7(rgyud): kyis tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bu la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// shA ri'i bu legs so legs so// shA ri'i bu khyod 'di ltar theg pa chen po la yang dag par bzhugs
16a8(rgyud): pa dang / theg pa chen po la mngon par brtson pa dang / theg pa chen po la lhag par byed pa dag la/ khyod gzungs yul na mi gnas/ phyogs mi gnas par ston/
16b1(rgyud): pa yang legs so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ shA ri'i bu gzungs ni chos nyid kyis 'das pa ma yin/ ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba ma yin te/ shA ri'i bu gzungs ni 'das
16b2(rgyud): pa zhes mi 'chad/ ma 'ongs pa zhes mi 'chad/ da ltar byung ba zhes mi 'chad/ dngos por mi 'chad/ dngos po med par mi 'chad/ mtshan ma dang / mtshan ma med
16b3(rgyud): par mi 'chad/ chos gang yang skye ba 'am/ 'gag pa'i phyir mi 'chad mod kyi/ shA ri'i bu 'on kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams la phan par gzhed pa'i phyir ston te/
16b4(rgyud): gang 'di gzungs kyi chos kyi rnams grangs kyi gzungs ni gzugs med pa/ bya ba'i lam du gyur pa/ rigs pa'i stobs kyi gnas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan/
16b5(rgyud): sangs rgyas kyi lhag par bya ba sgrub pa/ sangs rgyas kyi tshul khrims/ sangs rgyas kyis bsdus pa/ sangs rgyas kyi 'tshams sbyor ba/ sangs rgyas 'byung ba'o//
16b6(rgyud): de nas tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bus/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das gzungs gang la gnas shing gzungs de thob na/ byang chub
16b7(rgyud): sems dpa' bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyi mi ldog par 'gyur ba dang / dam bcas pa bzang ba dang / chos la mi gnas pa dang / bdag la
16b8(rgyud): the tshom ma mchis pa dang / slob pa ma mchis pa dang / rang gi lam la gnas pa bcom ldan 'das bshad du gsol/ bde bar gshegs pas bshad du gsol/
17a1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ shA ri'i bu legs so legs so// shA ri'i bu gzungs thob pa'i byang chub sems
17a2(rgyud): dpa' ni/ sangs rgyas nyid du brjod do// shA ri'i bu gang la la zhig byang chub sems dpa' gzungs thob pa la sti stang byed dam/ bla mar byed dam/ rim gror byed dam/
17a3(rgyud): mchod par byed dam/ des sangs rgyas thams cad la dad la ste stang byas par 'gyur ro// gang dag gis gzungs thob pa dang / gang dag mos pa de dag kyang sangs rgyas
17a4(rgyud): rnams ji lta ba de bzhin du mchod pa'i 'os su 'gyur zhing / byang chub kyi sems dang mi 'bral bar 'gyur ro// shA ri'i bu gzungs ni 'di yin te/ san d+ha ra ni/
17a5(rgyud): ud da ta ra na/ sam pra ti shA ta/ su ta ma/ su pra ti sha tA/ bI tsa ya be la/ a b+ha pra ti da na nya/ a ro ha/ d+hA na ba ti/ ud ba ti ni/ ba na mA ni/ a b+hiSh+Ta
17a6(rgyud): nita.a b+hi bya ha ra/ shu b+ha be ti/ a ni shi tra/ a ba hu ku b+ha/ a b+hi ba tsa// shA ri'i bu 'di dag ni dbang bskur ba'i gzungs kyi tshig rnams te/ 'das pa
17a7(rgyud): rnams dang / ma 'ongs rnams dang / da ltar byung ba rnams dang / legs par gnas pa rnams byang chub sems dpa' gang gis lags par bzung ste 'chang ba dang /
17a8(rgyud): myur du mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par bya ba'i phyir bskal pa brgyad dang / bskal pa stong dag smon lam gyis zad par bgyid par 'gyur/ de la mtshon gyis
17b1(rgyud): tshugs par mi 'gyur/ me dang srog chags mi bsrun pa rnams kyis tshugs par mi 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di lta ste rigs kyi bu gzungs 'di ni 'das pa'i
17b2(rgyud): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yum mo// ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi yum mo// shA ri'i bu rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu me/
17b3(rgyud): gang la las/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po grangs med pa bcu mthar chags su gang ba'i sangs rgyas rnams la na bza' dang / zhal zas bzang pos bskal pa grangs
17b4(rgyud): med par bzung bar bya bas rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gzhan gang gis gzung 'di las tha na tshig gam cig tsam bzung ba/ de bas ches bsod nams mang du bskyed//
17b5(rgyud): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sha ri'i bu dbang bskur ba'i gzungs 'di ni/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yum yin pa'i phyir ro// bcom ldan 'das kyi de skad ces bka' stsal nas//
17b6(rgyud): dge slong deg dang / byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang / lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
17b7(rgyud): gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// 'phags pa dbang bskur ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs rdzogs so// / rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya aSh+Ta maN+Da la kan na ma ma hA
17b8(rgyud): ya na sU tra/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa dkyil 'khor brgyad pa zhes bya ba'i theg pa chen po'i mdo// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag
18a1(rgyud): 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das ri gru 'dzin na 'phags pa spyan ras
18a2(rgyud): gzigs dbang phyug gis gnas na byang chub sems dpa' 'bum phrag du ma dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs te/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
18a3(rgyud): rin po chen snying po zla ba snang ba zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor de nyid du 'dus par gyur te 'dug pa stan las langs nas/ chos gos phrag pa gcig tu
18a4(rgyud): bzar te/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces
18a5(rgyud): gsol to// gal zhus na zhu ba lung bstan pa'i slad du/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bdag la skabs phye na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom
18a6(rgyud): ba yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la bdag phyogs 'ga' zhig zhu'o// de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' sems
18a7(rgyud): dpa' chen po rin chen snying po bzla ba la 'ding skad ces bka' stsal to// rin chen sring po zla ba snang ba khyod/ ci dang ci 'dod pa dris shig dang / ngas dris pa de dang de
18a8(rgyud): lung bstan pas/ khyod kyi sems rengs par bya'o// de skad ces bka' stsal ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rin chen snying po zla ba snang bas/
18b1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang la la/ dkyil 'khor brgyad bgyid par 'tshal na des ji ltar bgyi/
18b2(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu khyod skye bo mang po la shin du phan pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / dus gsum du skye ba'i sems can rnams kyi mtshungs
18b3(rgyud): ba med pa'i ye shes bsgrub pa'i phyir/ rigs kyi bu khyod kyi spobs pa ni bzang te/ legs so legs so// rigs kyi bu de'i phyir snying po gang brjod pa tsam gyis/ mtshams
18b4(rgyud): med pa lnga byang zhing / dngos grub thams cad kyang thobs par gyur pa/ byang chub sems dpa' brgyad kyi snying po nyon cig/ oM hu 'um ma hA bi re swA hA/ snying po 'dis ni
18b5(rgyud): dbus kyi bcom ldan 'das mchod do// oM hriH/ hu 'um pad ma pri yA ya swA hA/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi snying po'o// oM swa hA ra na swA hA/ byams
18b6(rgyud): pa'i snying po'o// oM A kha garbe swA hA/ na mkha'i snying po'i snying po'o// oM sA hri rdzi ya swA hA/ kun tu bzang po'i snying po'o// oM ku ru rba na hA ra swA hA/ lag na rdo rje
18b7(rgyud): snying po'o// oM shrI AM raM ga swA hA/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i snying po'o// oM ni sI raM ba swA hA/ sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba'i snying po'o// oM
18b8(rgyud): k+Shi ti hA rA dze swA hA/ sa'i snying po'i snying po'o// byang chub sems dpa' brgyad kyi snying po de bzhin gshegs pa dang ldan pa 'di/ rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang
19a1(rgyud): la la zhig gis/ dkyil 'khor gyi mdun du lan gcig brjod na/ de'i don thams cad 'grub par
19a2(rgyud): 'gyur te/ myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/
19a3(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// 'phags pa dkyil 'khor brgyad pa
19a4(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i gzungs rdzogs so// / rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya ASh+Ta maN+Da d+harma bar+ya na ma ma hA ya na sU tra/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa dkyil 'khor brgyad pa
19a5(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs theg pa chen po'i mdo// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus cig na/
19a6(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal po brgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na/ dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge
19a7(rgyud): 'dun chen po dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs te/ lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye
19a8(rgyud): chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa du mas yongs su bskor te/ 'dun gyis ltas pa dang / chos ston to// de nas de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' seng ge'i rgyal po bkod
19b1(rgyud): pa zhes bya bar 'dus par gyur nas 'dug pa des 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor chen po de mthong nas ltad mor gyur te de stan las langs te bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar te/
19b2(rgyud): pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der logasu thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to//
19b3(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das bdag gis sangs rgyas byung ba bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du ma zhig 'das na gang gis 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yang bcom ldan 'das ci 'dra ba de 'dra
19b4(rgyud): bar ma gyur lags so// bcom ldan 'das bdag gis zhu ba bstan pa 'di'i lan srul tu gsol/ byang chub sems dpa' gzhan dag gis thos na yang dbugs byin
19b5(rgyud): par 'gyur lags so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor gzengs bstod pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' seng ge'i rgyal po bkod pa la
19b6(rgyud): 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu nyon cig dang / dris pa lan gdab pa dkyil 'khor brgyad pa zhes bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs yod de/ gang ngas sngon so
19b7(rgyud): so skye bo'i dus na/ bsten cing kun tu bsgoms te/ lan mang du byas pa de bstan par bya'o// rigs kyi bu sngon byung ba 'das pa'i dus na/ de bzhin gshegs pa
19b8(rgyud): dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas snang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhes bya ba bzhugs te/ 'tsho zhing gzhes la chos kyang ston to// de'i dus na drag shul
20a1(rgyud): can gyis byin zhes bya ba'i khyim bdag cig/ shin tu ma dad cing yid du mi 'ong ba'i chos lnga dang ldan pa/ chos 'dul
20a2(rgyud): ba la brgyab kyis phyogs so// dge slong rnam par rgyal ba 'byung ba zhes bya ba zhig khyim bdag de la snying brtse ba'i phyir/ yang dang yang du rgyun mi 'chad par khyim bdag de'i
20a3(rgyud): khyim du 'gro'o// re zhig na dus kyi mthus khyim bdag de dge slong de la rjes su chags pa dang bcas pa'i sems su gyur nas/ re zhig khyim bdag de legs par bya ba'i
20a4(rgyud): las kyi 'bras bu dris so// de nas dge slong des skye bo mang po la phan pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba'i phyir dang / 'jig rten la snying brtse ba'i phyir dang / lha dang ma/
20a5(rgyud): rnams kyi skye bo phal po che'i don dang / phan pa dang bde ba'i phyir khyim bdag de la/ dkyil 'khor brgyad ces bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs ston te/ khyim bdag dkyil
20a6(rgyud): 'khor brgyad ces bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs gang zhe na/ bde ba thams cad sbyin par byed pa'o// de'i 'khor phun sum tshogs pa thob par 'gyur te/ gang dang gang
20a7(rgyud): du skyes par chos dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams dang mi 'bral bar 'gyur/ 'khor mang po phun sum tshogs nas/ gzugs bzang po nyid thob par 'gyur/
20a8(rgyud): yo byed snyam tshogs par 'gyur te/ btsal mi dgos par yo byad rnams 'byor par 'gyur/ lus sra zhing brtan la lus phun sum tshogs pas thob par 'gyur zhing /
20b1(rgyud): de la ri dang brtsigs pa rnams sgrib par mi byed de/ phun sum tshogs pa bzhi po de dag thob par 'gyur ro// de nas khyim bdag de dga' zhing mgu la yid rangs par
20b2(rgyud): gyur nas/ dge slong de'i rkang pa la phyag byas te 'di skad ces smras so// 'phags pa dkyil 'khor brgyad ston cig dang / des bdag la mngon sum du 'gyur ro//
20b3(rgyud): de nas dge slong rnam par rgyal ba 'byung bas/ khyim bdag de'i bsam pa shes nas yang dag par rab tu bstan te/ rigs kyi bu nyon cig dang bstan par bya'o// des ni
20b4(rgyud): lci bar bsred pa yi/ dkyil 'khor grwa bzhi lham par bya/ sems can kun dang thun mong du/ 'das pa'i sangs rgyas gang yin dang / gang dag ma 'ongs da ltar byung /
20b5(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dag gang yod pa/ de dag rnams la yongs su bsngo// de nas dkyil 'khor 'khor yug tu/ 'khor gyi dkyil
20b6(rgyud): 'khor rnams bya ste/ 'jig rten dbang dang byams pa dang / thub pa skye mchog na mkha' dang / kun tu bzang po blo ldan dang / de bzhin gsang ba'i bdag po dang / 'jam
20b7(rgyud): dpal gzhon nur gyur pa dang / sgrib pa thams cad rnam sel dang / de bzhin sa'i snying po'o// de dag gi ched du dkyil 'khor brgyad pa'o// khyim bdag 'di ni dkyil
20b8(rgyud): 'khor brgyad ces bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs yin te/ 'di ni bdag gis bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa snang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa de las mngon sum du
21a1(rgyud): zos so// khyim bdag gzhan yang nyon cig/ kun nas bskal pa mthun pa yi/ 'khor rnams gang zhig 'dod pa des/ dkyil
21a2(rgyud): 'khor brgyad ni bri bar bya/ gang zhig brgya byin nyid dang ni/ tshangs pa'i 'jig rten bdag po dang / lha mi rgyal po'i rgyal srid dang / blo ldan sna tshogs gzugs bzang 'dod
21a3(rgyud): rtag tu dkyil 'khor mchog brgyad bya/ seng ge'i rgyal po bkod pa 'di ji snyam du sems/ de'i tshe dge slong rnam par rgyal ba 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i de gzhan zhig yin snyam du
21a4(rgyud): 'dzin na de de ltar mi lta ste/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa 'di de'i tshe dus na/ dge slong rnam par rgyal ba 'byung ba zhes bya bar gyur to// seng ge'i rgyal po bkod pa
21a5(rgyud): de'i tshe de'i dus na khyim bdag drag shul can gyis byin pa zhes bya ba ste gzhan zhig yin snyam du som nyid 'am yid gnyis za na de ltar mi lta'o// nga nyid de'i tshe de'i dus na//
21a6(rgyud): drag shul na can gyis byin pa zhes bya ba'i khyim bdag du gyur to// ngas pha rol du phyin pa drug yongs su rdzogs par byas pa'i bar dang / sangs rgyas nyid thob kyi bar dang /
21a7(rgyud): sangs rgyas nyid thob kyi bar du tshe rabs bye ba khrag khrig phrag 'bum de dang de dag tu chos 'di kun du bsten to// bsgoms so// mya ngan du byas so/ rigs kyi bu gang gi
21a8(rgyud): na nga'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor bkod pa 'di 'dra bar gyur pa'i rgyu ni de yin no// rkyen ni de yin no// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ byang chub
21b1(rgyud): sems dpa' seng ge'i rgyal po bkod pa dang / dge slong de dag dang / byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang / thams cad dang ldan pa 'khor de dag dang / lha dang / me dang /
21b2(rgyud): lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// 'phags pa dkyil 'khor brgyad pa zhes
21b3(rgyud): bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs/ theg pa chen po'i mdo rdzogs s+ho// // rgya gar skad du/ ma hA g+ha na pa ti tan tra nA ma/ bod skad du/ tshogs
21b4(rgyud): kyi bdag po chen po'i rgyud ces bya ba/ 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas dpal ldan tshogs bdag che/ phyag 'tshal tshogs bdag dpal
21b5(rgyud): ldan dges/ gzugs brnyan dkyil 'khor gru bzhir bzhag/ zla ba drug tu mchod par bya/ lha yi 'khor los bsgyur ba dang / tshe ring bar bgyid bskal par mnyam/
21b6(rgyud): tshe ring ba yi mchog tu 'gyur/ mi la sogs pa dbang du 'gyur/ lha yi bu yang bran bzhin du/ bdag gi sgo ba nyan par 'gyur/ klu yang de bzhin bsgo ba nyan/
21b7(rgyud): bran bzhin las rnams 'byed par 'gyur/ lha yi longs spyod mnga' ris las/ 'dod pa'i longs spyod 'byung bar 'gyur/ dngos grub grub pa'i dbang phyug can/
21b8(rgyud): gdul bya'i dbang gi sgo sprul nas/ lha chen tshogs bdag chen por bya/ dngos grub dam pa mchog grub na/ mthu stobs phun sum chog ldan zhing / longs
22a1(rgyud): spyod yid bzhin 'phel bar byed/ 'jig rten 'phen mdzad lha yi lnga/ gang gi mchod pa'i dngos grub yin/ lha chen po
22a2(rgyud): tshogs kyi bdag po'i rgyud las/ dngos grub 'byung ba'i le'u ste dang po'o// // de nas dben pa'i gnas su ni/ dkyil 'khor gru bzhi par byas te/
22a3(rgyud): ba pi lci bas legs par byugs/ 'jam zhing snyoms la dbus mtho ba/ dbus su tshogs bdag sku gzugs bzhag/ me tog dkar pos des la mchod/
22a4(rgyud): me tog dkar pos tshem bu bkod/ bdag nyid gcer bur byas nas ni/ log 'dren gzugs bris yang dag mchod/ ba ra ta ka zla drug/ nyin re bzhin du dus
22a5(rgyud): gsum du/ gsang sngags brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas na/ yid la re ba kun rdzogs byed/ bsam pa thams cad 'grub par 'gyur/ oM ni bkra shis dpal dang ldan/
22a6(rgyud): gsang sngags mgo la bzhag par bya/ yid bzhin nor bu lta bu yis/ dngos grub ster ba'i yi ge dang / de'i 'og gral la bzhag par bya/ nyi ma lta bu'i yi ge
22a7(rgyud): yang / de'i rjes la bsgrags par bya/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dang po/ pi ge'i mchog ni blang bar bya/ gsal byed yi ge drang po yang / kun gyi 'jus la
22a8(rgyud): brjod par bya/ rin chen yi ge swa zhes bya/ las kyi yi ge ha zhes bya/ dngos grub 'dod pas gsangs sngags bzlas/ lha chen po'i dngos grub 'byung ba'i
22b1(rgyud): rgyud las/ lha'i dngos grub kyi gsangs sngags bstan pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// / de nas tshogs kyi bdag po bshad par bya ste/ tshogs kyi bdag po sku
22b2(rgyud): mdog dkar po glang po che'i mgo bo can/ mche ba ya tsag chag pa/ phyag na la bug dang / la tus gang ba'i snod bsnams pa/ bye ba la tshabs pa/ rin po ches sku
22b3(rgyud): brgyan pa/ zla ba ches pa'i dbu brgyan can/ 'od gsal ba/ 'od 'phro ba/ mdog bzang ba/ kha dog bzang ba/ gsus pa che ba/ brgyan gyi sprad pa'o// dngos grub
22b4(rgyud): 'byung ba'i rgyud las/ tshogs kyi bdag po bstan pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// / de nas skar ma rgyal gyi nyin par me tog dkar ba'i shing gi rtsa ba blangs
22b5(rgyud): te/ tshegs kyi bdag po'i gzugs bya ste/ kha dogs dkar po glang po che'i mgo can/ phyag g.yas na la phug dang / g.yon na nor bu rin po che'i bsnams pa'o//
22b6(rgyud): lcags mas dgra sta dang / kha T+wAM ka rnam pa/ gsus pa che ba brgyan thams cad kyis brgyan pa/ zla ba dang byi ba'i khri la zhugs pa mkhas pas byas so// de dkyil 'khor
22b7(rgyud): gyi dbus su bdag la zhal mngon par phyogs pas bzhag la/ bdag nyid log 'dren gyis gzugs kyi yang dag par mchod do// tshogs kyi bdag po zhal cig phyag bzhi
22b8(rgyud): ba grub/ de nas dbang ldan gyi mtshams su/ tshogs kyi bdag po glang po che'i mgo can/ byi ba la chibs pa/ mig gsum pa/ zla ba phyed pa 'dzin pa/
23a1(rgyud): g.yas na la pug dang dgra sta 'dzin cing / g.yon pa dag na tri shA la dang thod pa 'dzin pa'o// lag pa g.yon pa khu tshur
23a2(rgyud): bcangs pa las/ 'dzum mo dang gung mo brkyang la/ 'dzub mo bkug la mgung mo'i tshigs su gzugs par bya ba ni tshogs kyi bdag po'i phyag rgya'o// tshogs kyi bdag
23a3(rgyud): po'i phyag rgya brtan pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// / de nas bsang sngags bstan pa ni/ oM ni dpal dang mgo la bzhag/ de nas yid bzhin nor bu ni/ rin po che'i
23a4(rgyud): yi ge bri/ sde tshan gsal byed dang po yang / de yi rjes su bri bar bya/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dang po// dbyang yig brgyad pas mdzes par bya/ gsal byed dang pe'i
23a5(rgyud): yi ge yang / blo yi blangs te yid kyi bri/ sde tshan bzhi pa'i gsum pa la/ dang po'i lnga pas sbyar bar bya/ sde tshan bdun pa'i dang po la/ gsum pa'i dang po'i 'og tu sbyar/
23a6(rgyud): yid bzhin nor bu'i yi ge la/ bzhi pa'i lnga pa zla la bzhag/ dbyangs yig gsum pas brgyan par bya/ bzhi pa'i bzhi pa de nas brjod/ dngos grub bsgrubs pa'i
23a7(rgyud): yi ge ni/ de yi rjes la bri bar bya/ gsang sngags drag po'i yi ge yang / kun gyi mthar ni brjod par bya/ gsang sngags 'di yid dngos grub ni/ 'jig rten
23a8(rgyud): dbang phyug nyid kyi byin/ dgos pa thams cad sgrub pa'o// tshogs bdag chen po'i gsang sngags bstan pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// // de nas gzhan
23b1(rgyud): yang gsungs pa ni/ dngos grub thams cad sgrub pa ni/ mtshan gyi gsang sngags zhes bya ba/ dngos grub 'grub pa'i snying po ni/ dpal ldan dbyangs kyi yi ge ste/
23b2(rgyud): oM zhes bya ba mgo la bzhag/ yid bzhin nor bu'i yi ge la/ nyi mi'i yi ge 'og tu sbas/ dbyangs yig drag po 'og tu sbyar/ thig le des ni brgyan par bya'o//
23b3(rgyud): mtshan gyi dang po'i yi ge ni/ de yi rjes la brjod par bya/ bzhi pa'i lnga pa de nas par/ lnga pa'i dang po bri bar bya/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dang po// de yis
23b4(rgyud): rjes la brjod par bya/ 'byung ba rlung gi yi ge la/ dbyangs yig brgyad pas brgyan pa ni/ de yis rjes la bri bar bya// bzhi pa'i yig 'bru gnyis po yang /
23b5(rgyud): kun gyi mthar ni brjod par bya/ mtshan gyi gsang sngags zhes bya ba/ 'dod pa thams cad sgrub byed yin/ mtshan gyi gsang sngags bstan pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o//
23b6(rgyud): / de nas yang dag bshad bya ba/ skar ma rgyal gyi nyin par ni/ me tog dkar po'i rtsa ba 'am/ tsan dan dkar po dag las ni/
23b7(rgyud): tshogs kyi bdag po'i sku gzugs ni/ the bong gi ni tshad tsam bya/ gsus po che ba phyag bzhi pa/ mkhas pas byas te legs pa ni/ rin po che yi snod du bzhag/
23b8(rgyud): skar chen mngon par gsal ba'i tshe/ nang gi cha rigs ska khrus gsol/ gtsang zhing dang la yid du 'ong / dri dang ldan pa'i bum pa 'dis/ me tog dkar po dri yi ni/
24a1(rgyud): 'dag 'tshal ldan pas khrus bya'o// de nas de ma thag tu ni/ dkyil 'khor dbus su spyan drangs te/ me tog dkar
24a2(rgyud): po dbul bar bya/ la bug la dur bcas pa yi/ gtor ma chen po de nas dbul/ spos dang dri dang mar me dang / lha bshos dag gis mchod par bya/ gsang
24a3(rgyud): sngags 'dis la phug dang / de nas du dang / chu dang phye dang bcas pa'i dkar gsum gyi gtor mtshogs kyi bdag po la dbul te/ spos dang me togs kyang de ltar phul nas/
24a4(rgyud): de'i phyir bgegs byed par mi nus so// tshegs kyi bdag po mchod pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// / de nas la phug zhes bya ba/ ro dang ldan pa'i nyung ma ste/
24a5(rgyud): zas rnams kun gyi mchog kyang yin/ ro mchog brgyad dang ldan pa yin/ kha dang skyur dang bska ba dang / dngar dang tshwa dang lan tshe ro// bzhun dang ro mchog che ba yin/
24a6(rgyud): nad ni brgyad kyi gnyen po yin/ 'khris pa bad kan 'dus pa dang / khrag dang chu sor ma zhu ba/ rlung dang rim nad kun la pan/ 'di 'byung po'i kha zas te/ lha rnams kun
24a7(rgyud): gyis mthu yang stsol/ dngos grub 'grub pa'i zhal zas yin/ tshogs kyi bdag po mchog par bya/ la du zhes bya'i zhal zas ni/ mngar gsum 'bras bu gsum pa dang /
24a8(rgyud): de bzhin zhim pa'i spos kyi bran/ bag zam gang du ril bu pa/ 'o ma mar du bcos la bya/ tshogs pa'i gtor ma chen po dang / mar dang khur ba dkar gsum dang /
24b1(rgyud): mthun pa'i zhal zas sna tshogs kyis/ tshogs kyi bdag po mchod par bya'o// de ltar tshogs bdag po la mchod pa phul nas/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i sku gzugs lag pa
24b2(rgyud): g.yas pa'i 'thil du bzhugs nas/ sems gzhan du ma yengs pas bzlas brjod 'bum byas na/ rnal 'byor pa bam par mi 'gyur ro// ma'i nang na bsod nams chung ba
24b3(rgyud): yin na yang / bzlas brjod 'bum byas te la phug la sngags kyis btabs te tshogs kyi bdag po la mchod na/ tshe 'di nyid la 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po dang bsod
24b4(rgyud): nams mnyam par 'gyur ro// me tog dkar pos mchod na rgyal po la sogs pas pham mi 'gyur ro// rgyal po dang blon po la sogs pa bdag gi dbang du 'gyur ro//
24b5(rgyud): dngos grub sgrub pa'i rdzas bstan pa'i le'u ste brgyad pa'o// / de nas ga gzhan bshad bya/ dngul zhes bya ba'i rin chen las/ tshegs bdag chen
24b6(rgyud): po'i gzugs byas te/ yid bzhin ron bu lag na thogs/ dkyil 'khor chen po gru gang tshad/ rin chen me togs dkar po bkram/ gsang sngags 'bum du bzlas pa byas/
24b7(rgyud): nad dang sdug bsngal zhi bar byas/ shel dang dngul las tshogs ske/ mkhas pas ji ltar 'byor pa bya/ sdug bsngal thams cad sel bar 'gyur/ rin chen shel
24b8(rgyud): las tshogs bdag ska/ mthe bong tsam gyi tshad du bya/ pra se na zhes bya ba'i sngags/ rig pa 'bum du bzlas byas te/ shel gyi skra de khrus byas nas//
25a1(rgyud): ska ma rgyal gyi nyan par ni/ bdag nyid shar du kha bltas te/ gos dkar gyon nas khrus byas te/ thal sbyar yid
25a2(rgyud): kyi gsol ba btab/ bdag la gnod pa'i bgegs gang yin/ shel gyi skra de me long la/ me long gang la gsal bar 'gyur/ yang na se na pra zhes pa'i/
25a3(rgyud): rigs pa'i rgyal mo 'bum du bzlas/ shel gyi skra de me long ste/ mi g.yo mi 'gul bar ni bzhag/ bdag nyid shar byas shar du lta/ rtso ra ba dang rkun me ni/
25a4(rgyud): gang yin me long nang du 'byung / de tshe de'i de ngos zin/ tshogs bdag shel gyi sku de ni/ mchod nas rab gnas legs byas nas/ nam ku ru zhes bya ba yi/ rigs pa
25a5(rgyud): 'bum du bzlas byas nas/ nad dang sdug bsngal gyis nyen la/ skra de bstan pa tsam gyis ni/ nad pa rnams kyang sos par 'gyur/ sdug bsngal las kyang thar par
25a6(rgyud): 'gyur/ zhi ba'i cho ga chen po yin/ rin chen gser zhes bya ba las/ tshogs bdag chen po'i sku byas te/ mchod dang bzlas brjod brtson byas nas/ skye ba 'di dang
25a7(rgyud): phyi ma la/ rtag tu yo byad 'phel bar 'gyur/ nor gyi bdag po rnam thos bu/ rgyal po bzhin du bsnyen bkur byed/ des nas dpal ldan tshogs bdag gi/ sku gzugs
25a8(rgyud): dkyil 'khor gru bzhir bzhag/ ba ra ta pa'i gsang sngags ni/ bzlas pa 'bum du byas pa yis/ tshe 'di nyid la dngos grub ni/ ci dang ci 'dod sbyin pa mdzad//
25b1(rgyud): lha yi rgyal po'i mnga' zang ni/ sgrub pa po la rtsol bar mdzad/ shin tu thugs rje'i bdag nyid las/ dpal ldan tshogs bdag thugs rje che/ thug rje chen pos dbul
25b2(rgyud): ba bskyobs/ nor lha chen po'i bdag nyid 'di/ dar ram ra sa la legs bris te/ rgyal gyi nyin par spyan phye nas/ gang gi khyim du bzhugs pa yi/ sa phyogs de ni
25b3(rgyud): bkra shis 'gyur/ zangs las tshogs bdag chen po'i sku/ mkhas pas legs par bzo byas nas/ tsan dan dmar pos byugs pa phi/ maN+Dal steng du legs
25b4(rgyud): bar bzhag/ ban tu ka'i me tog dang / pad ma rA ga rin chen dang / me tog dmar po kun gyis mchod/ b+h+rU~M zhes bya ba'i reg pa bzlas/ rgyal po'i bu mo dbang du
25b5(rgyud): 'gyur/ lha mo klu mo mi mo dang / mi 'am ci'i bu mo dang / bram ze'i bu mo mtshan ldan pa/ mchog tu gzugs bzang 'gugs par 'gyur/ bran mo'i bzhin du bsgo
25b6(rgyud): ba nyan/ de la sogs pa mtha' yas mchog/ sku gzugs dag la bsten te mchog/ mchod pa tsam gyi 'byung ba yin/ gzhan yang tshogs bdag chen po'i sku/
25b7(rgyud): rin po che'i rgyu las byas/ dkyil 'khor steng du bzhugs byas te/ rat+na sing ti zhes bya ba'i/ rig pa 'bum du bzlas pa yis/ sa 'og gter rnams ston
25b8(rgyud): par byed/ ci dga' bar yang spyod par 'gyur/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i rgyud las/ rgyal po la sogs pa sgrub pa'i le'u ste dgu pa'o// /
26a1(rgyud): de nas dpal ldan tshegs bdag che/ drag po chen po drag shul can/ sangs rgyas thugs la byol song dbu/ gla rkyen gzhu nas
26a2(rgyud): zhal brgyan pa/ spyan gsum che ba bzhi dang ldan/ phyag bzhi pa zhabs gnyis klu chen mnan/ dang po mche ba dkar po 'dzin/ de 'og gzhags pa g.yon pa na/ dgra
26a3(rgyud): lta khA tri rtse gsum 'dzin/ 'thing kha gsus pa 'byang ba'o// de lta bu'i tshogs bdag sku/ 'khar ba 'am khro chu dag la bya/ rgyal gyi nyin par rab tu gnas/ de nas
26a4(rgyud): sgom zhing sgrub pa yi/ dkyil 'khor bya ba'i sa stegs la/ le rtse dgu yi 'khor lo bri/ sgo dang mu khyud ldan par bri/ dbus su pad ma 'dab brgyad la/ tshogs bdang
26a5(rgyud): chen po sgrub bya mnan/ zla ba'i gdan la yum dang ni/ gnyis su med par bkod par bya/ de ming la rtse ka ra te/ rdo rje phag me'i sngo zhes bya/ dgra sta ban d+ha lag na
26a6(rgyud): thogs/ khrag gis bkang ba gtse la stobs/ shar gyi le rtse ser po la khams/ gsum gyi bdag po ser po// phub dang dgra 'dzin pa'o// lho phyogs le rtse sngon po/
26a7(rgyud): gnod sbyin chen po chu ma he'i gdong can/ dbyugs pa dang thod pa 'dzin pa'o// nub kyi le rtse dmar po la gnod sbyin gyi bdag po sprin gyi bdag po zhes bya ba/ chus gang
26a8(rgyud): ba'i sprin phung dang / zhags pa 'dzin pa dkar po'o// byang phyogs kyi le rtse ljang khra la/ gnod sbyin gyi bdag po nor gnas zhes bya ba/ dbyug to dang rin po che
26b1(rgyud): rdzogs pa ser po'o/ byang shar gyi le tse dkar po la/ 'byung po'i bdag po dkar po// rtse gas pa dang sngags 'dra ba bas shang k+ko le rtse dmang po la/ yid dgas pa rgyal
26b2(rgyud): bo drag po zhes bya ba dgra sta dang / mi'i thod pa bas ril thogs pa nag po'o// lho nub kyi le rtse nag po la/ sprin gyi sgron ma lag na sprin bung dang / klog gi 'od du bcas
26b3(rgyud): ba lag pa gnyis kyi thogs pa'o// nub byang gi le tse nag po la/ bgegs kyi bdag po log 'dren sna yon zhes bya ba/ glang po che'i sna can rtse gsum dang thod pa skam po'i nang du
26b4(rgyud): la phug dang shas bkang ba thogs pa'o// lha rnams la klu'i rgyal po brgyad thal mo sbyar nas bka' nyan pa ni/ klu'i rgyal po a ba la dang / ba ru na dang / drang skyong dang /
26b5(rgyud): 'jog po dang / rigs ldan dang / mtha' yas dang / pad ma dang / pad ma chen po rnams so// shar phyogs kyi sgor rgyal po chen po yul 'khor bsrung / lho sgor bag
26b6(rgyud): skyes po// nub sgor byin mi bzang / byang sgor rnam thos sras/ sku mdog dkar po dang / sngon po dang / ljang khra rnams rim par shes par bya'o// lag na nor bu rin
26b7(rgyud): po che re re dang / ral gri re re 'dzin pa'o// de rnams kyi chung ma ni bri mi dgos so// de ltar bris pa'i dkyil 'khor de'i byang shar mtshams su gsad pa'i dkyil 'khor
26b8(rgyud): gru gsum brus la de'i nang du dgra gzugs pra tshil las byas te ring ba mdog nag po// skra ser ba/ lus til mar gyi byug pa byas te/ snying khar ming dang rus
27a1(rgyud): bris la bzhug go// de'i skye nas ro'i skra las thag pa byas te gdags par bya'o// de ltar byas nas gnod sbyin chen po
27a2(rgyud): la/ la du dang la phug tu byas pa'i gtor ma dang / gnod sbyin chen po brgyad la nya sha dang sgog cong du sbyar ba'i gtor ma re re bsham/ klu chen brgyad la gtor ma chen po
27a3(rgyud): gcig/ rgyal po chen po chen bzhi la re re bya'o// gal te ma 'byor na gtor ma chen po gcig bya'o// lha bshos re re dbul bar bya'o// gzhan yang drag po'i rdzas
27a4(rgyud): l+le spyang gi thod pa dang / zing nag po dang / kye tshe dang / nyung kar nag po bzhag par bya'o// tshogs bdag chen po'i drag po'i dkyil 'khor bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu pa'o//
27a5(rgyud): / de nas gzhan yang bshad bya ba/ bsgom pa'i rim pa 'di lta bu/ ma byung 'byung bar mi 'gyur bas/ shin tu gsang ste
27a6(rgyud): sgrub par bya/ a yi rang bzhin stong pa las/ snang ba'i rang bzhin hUM dang ni/ ya tshegs brgyad pa'i sa bon 'byung / ming gi sngags las rab tu skyes/ khro
27a7(rgyud): bo'i sprul pas stong gsum gang / 'od zer 'dus pa'i gzugs la 'dzud/ tshogs kyi bdag po chen po ste/ 'gro ba'i don du bzhengs pa ni/ khro bo chen po 'jig
27a8(rgyud): pa'i gzugs/ yum dang 'khor yang rdzogs par bskyed/ phuHbrgyad klu brgyad sems pa'i tshul/ rgyal po sde bzhi khro bo'i tshul raShA da ni bye ru dang / bai dang
27b1(rgyud): khe ru'i ming las skyes/ 'od zer tshul gyi spyan drang ba/ dza dang dza'i 'bro 'dra dang / hA dang hU~M gi gsang sngags dang / lcags kyu'i phyag rgyas spyan drangs la/ nus pa
27b2(rgyud): mthu dang ldan par bya/ mchod dang gtor ma btab par bya/ ba ling gri h+Na gri ha na/ kha kha khA hi khA hi'i sngags/ snying po dag dang spel bar bya/ bsgom pa'i rim pa'i le'u
27b3(rgyud): ste bcu gcig pa'o// / de nas gsang sngags rgyal po ni/ dbyangs dang gsal byed las btu/ oM ni sum tshogs pa ste/ sngags kyi mgo la
27b4(rgyud): bzhag par bya/ bzhi pa'i snga pa de rjes bri/ gsal byed lnga pa'i lnga pa btu/ dang po'i bzhi pa de rjes bris/ bzhi pa'i lnga pa gral la bzhag/ yid bzhin nor bu'i yi ge yang /
27b5(rgyud): de'i rjes su bzhag par bya/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dang po// de yi rjes su brjod par bya/ de la dbyangs yig brgyad pas brgyan/ 'gug pa'i yi ge ni dang ni/
27b6(rgyud): 'byung ba rlung gi yi ge la/ dbyangs yig gnyis pa sbyar ba yis/ rgyal ba'i rgyal po zhes brjod do// yin bzhin nor bu'i yi ge la/ dbyangs yid gnyis pa sbyar
27b7(rgyud): bar bya/ nyi ma yi ni yi ge la/ bzhi pa'i lnga pa de nas bris/ de la dbyangs yig brgyad pas brgyan/ gnyis pa bzhi pa'i yi ge la/ dbyangs yig bzhi pas brgyan
27b8(rgyud): bar bya/ lnga pa bzhi pa'i yi ge la/ gsum pa'i lnga pas sbyar bar bya/ bzhi pa dang po'i yi ge la/ dbyangs kyi bzhi pas brgyan par bya/ 'byung ba rlung gi yi ge yang /
28a1(rgyud): de yi 'og tu sbyar bar bya/ rin po che'i yi ge dang / las kyi yi ge'i tha mar brjod/ tshogs bdag chen po'i rtsa ba'i
28a2(rgyud): sngags/ 'dod pa thams cad sgrub byed yin/ gnod sbyin brgyad kyi gsang sngags ni/ ya zhes bya ba la sogs pa dang / ba zhes bya ba dang / k+Sha zhes bya ba la sogs pa dang /
28a3(rgyud): be na ya ka zhes bya ba la sogs pa dang / be zhes bya ba dang / ra zhes bya ba dang / tri zhes bya ba ste brgyad las/ hI dang phaT kyis mtha' rten pa ni/ srog gis snying
28a4(rgyud): po'o// klu yi sngags ni ming las kyis/ oM dang phaT dang ldan par bya/ rgyal po'i gsang sngags ni/ be zhes bya ba dang bi zhes bya ba dang / nga zhes bya ba dang / ba zhes
28a5(rgyud): bya ba'i sngags su 'gyur ro// gnod sbyin chen po rnams kyis gsang sngags kyi le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o// / bsgrub bya 'gugs pa'i gsang sngags
28a6(rgyud): ni/ la dang sha dang ka dang la/ ma dang d+ha dang b+ha dang b+he/ tri dang ra dang tsa dag gis/ sha tr-i ne dza ne dza/ zhes len grangs mang du bzlas par bya'o// gnod sbyin brgyad
28a7(rgyud): kyi gsang sngags kyi dgra bo'i bla rdo bgrang bar bya'o// sngon du oM na ma ka ka pa ri stong bzlas pa'i rtags ni/ til gyi ling ka 'grul/ de nas bla rdo bsrag por bya/
28a8(rgyud): de nas bla rdo bsreg par bya/ de nas bla rdo mnan par bya/ rbad pa'i gsang sngags rgyal po ni/ ya dang kA dang ka la dang / ma dang hA dang b+he ra b+he/ de ba yak+Sha ma ma dang /
28b1(rgyud): na ga na ga zum ril yA/ dgra bo che gaM thum ril ya/ ya ya ces kyang bskul bar bya/ de nas gsang ba'i gsang sngags ni/ ma dang ha dang b+he ra b+he/ yak+Sha la sogs
28b2(rgyud): gong dang mthun/ de rjes 'di skad brjod par bya/ nag lan sha gnyis so// rdzun n+dan tra sa la/ na ga ya kA ma ra ye/ ha na tshin d+hu rim pa gnyis/ bi na ya ka dza~M bin
28b3(rgyud): ta/ an d+ha ka ra de nas brjod/ che ge ma ra ya zhes pa/ hUM hUM phaT phaT drag par ldan/ bsad pa'i gsang sngags bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu gsus pa'o//
28b4(rgyud): / de nas yang ni drag po'i sngags/ oM b+hi nA b+hi ma b+hi/ sarba b+har+ya ba sha ya/ hri ta b+hi ta ya/ hAM tsi tu ba tu/ tra ma ru ta ya/ ha na ha na/
28b5(rgyud): gr-i h+Na gri hA/ pa tsa ba tsa/ b+h+ra ma b+h+ra ma/ b+ha ma ya b+h+ra ma ya/ hUM hUM phaT phaT/ 'kha ba 'am ni zangs dag las/ log 'dren chen po'i sku gzugs bya/ de la
28b6(rgyud): rab gnas mchod pa bya/ dgra bo'i gzugs brnyen 'og tu gzhugs/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i gdan du bya/ dgra de 'chi bar the tshom med/ yang ni sbyor ba'i las
28b7(rgyud): rnams ni/ dgos pa chen po 'di gzungs so// tshogs kyi bdag po'i ska tsan dan nam/ rin po che las byas pa rab gnas byas mchod pa phul te/ ser ba gcod
28b8(rgyud): par 'dod na/ ser ba'i bdag po rlung lha dang chu lha'i gzugs byas te/ sprin dang 'brug gis gzugs byas la/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i gdan du gnas par bya
29a1(rgyud): bdag nyid kyi kyang mnan par bsams te/ hri ka tsakra ces pa la sogs pa'i sngags bzlas na/ ser ba gcod par 'gyur ro//
29a2(rgyud): nyungs kar phyogs bcur gtor bar bya'o// ser ba 'bebs par 'dod na/ chu dang sprin gyi dkyil 'khor mngon par bris te/ tshegs bdag chen po 'brug la zhen
29a3(rgyud): par bsgom te/ bdag gis bka' nyan par bsgoms te/ gsang ba'i rdzas sngags bye zangs phye gser bye 'bras bye dang gnas kyi chus spras te/ ji tsam 'dod par
29a4(rgyud): dbyibs che chung byas te/ ku ku khyi gu'i thod pa'i nang du blugs te sprin dgab par bya'o// ku ku'i thod pa la sngags bri bar bya'o// rim pa gsum du'o// rten gyi rdzas
29a5(rgyud): kyang bzhag par bya'o// rtsa sngags dang / gsang sngags kyi bzhugs la gdags par bya'o// b+h+rUM b+haM b+ha ri sha la phreM pro hri la hri la shar shar phe ba/ zhes bya ba la
29a6(rgyud): sogs pa'i gsang sngags 'bum phrag gcig bzlas pa dang / ka ka'i thod pa'i nang du ser ba sngon la bdun nam brgyad 'ong ngo // byung ba dgra'i yul du bskyal te/
29a7(rgyud): gsang sngags bzlogs te bzlas pas ser ba chen po 'bab bo// gal te mi 'bab na tshogs bdag chen po'i gzugs de/ dbu thur la bstan/ zhabs gyen la bstan
29a8(rgyud): la sngags bzlog nas bzlas pas/ dgra be'i yul gyi zhing dbus su bcug pa tsam gyis ser ba mod la bab te bya ka lan ta ka'i sgong tsam 'bab ste/ dmar po dbyibs
29b1(rgyud): sha ba'i rlig 'bras tsam yun ring du 'bab bo// lo thogs 'joms pa'i gsang sngags ni thA zhes pas bya'o// sku dang ka ka'i thod pas byung bar du/ nyi ma re re dbab pas
29b2(rgyud): dbyung bar bya'o// tshogs kyi bdag po'i sku la mchod pa dpral bar bya'o// gsang sngags kyang ma nor bar bcing ngo // rin po che'i 'phreng ba la brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas par bya'o//
29b3(rgyud): skra khrus gsol lo// bdag gis dkyil 'khor du bzhugs su gsol lo// de las sogs pa mtha' yas tshogs/ tshogs kyi bdag pos byed pa yi/ phyag 'tshal dpal
29b4(rgyud): ldan tshegs bdag che/ phyag 'tshal dpal ldan tshogs bdag dges/ phyag 'tshal dpal ldan zhi ba che/ phyag 'tshal dpal ldan khro bo che/ dngos grub 'byung ba'i rgyud
29b5(rgyud): las/ tshogs kyi bdag po la bstod pa'i le'u ste bcwa brgyad pa'o// // tshogs kyi bdag po'i rgyud las/ dngos grub 'byung ba'i rgyud ces bya ba rdzogs so//
29b6(rgyud): rgya gar gyis mkhan po de po ka ra shre dz+nyA nas 'jig rten gyi dngos grub kyi ched du/ rgya gar gyi yul nas bsgyur nas/ 'brong ston pa rgyal ba'i
29b7(rgyud): 'byung gnas la gnang ba yin no// rgyud 'dis bsam pa thams cad 'grub ces gsungs so// / rgya gar skad du/ ar+ya ga na pa ti hr-id ya/
29b8(rgyud): bod skad du/ 'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po'i snying po/ sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i
30a1(rgyud): dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das rgyal po'i khab na/ bya rgod phung po'i ri la/ dge slong nyis brgya lnga bcu'i dge slong gi dge
30a2(rgyud): 'dun chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sha stag dang thabs cig tu bzhugs te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la bka'
30a3(rgyud): stsal ba/ kun dga' bo gang la la/ tshogs kyi bdag po tshegs kyi dbang phyug gi snying po 'dzin na/ de'i las thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro// de bzung bas dgos
30a4(rgyud): pa thams cad 'grub cing / gsang sngags thams cad kyang dngos grub du 'gyur ro// tad+ya thA/ na mo sU te/ ma hA ga na pa ta ye/ ka Ta ka Ta/ ki Ti ki Te ku Ta ku Ta/
30a5(rgyud): ma Ta ma Ta/ da ra da ra/ gri rna grih+na/ d+ha ba d+ha ba/ dzam b+ha dza ma b+ha/ sa ma ya ma nu sa mA ra/ na mo stu ste/ ru tra ba tsa ni ye swA hA/ a b+ha tri b+hin d+huk+ShA b+ha/ tsit+ta ra na b+ha/
30a6(rgyud): sa ma ga chung ba/ mahA mA pa/ mahA ba la/ ma hA ba ti/ dany+dza ni gA/ pra ko pa pa saM/ tad+yathA/ oM ku ru ku ru/ mu ru mu ru/ tsu run ru/ na mo na ma swAH/
30a7(rgyud): kun dga' bo rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo 'am/ dge slong ngam/ dge slong ma 'am/ dge bsnyen nam/ dge bsnyen ma gang la la zhig gis/ tshogs bdag kyi bdag
30a8(rgyud): po// tshogs kyi dbang phyug gis snying po 'di bcom zhing / gsang sngags sgrub pa 'am/ dkon mchog gsum mchod du yul gzhan du 'gro 'am/ rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor
30b1(rgyud): du 'jug na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la me tog dang bdug pas mchod pa byas te/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i snying po 'di klag na las thams cad 'grub kyis/
30b2(rgyud): 'di la the tshom ma za shig/ 'thab pa dang / rtsod pa dang / khrag 'khrugs pa dang / g.yul 'khrug pa thams cad kyi nang du yang dran par byas nas thams cad rab tu zhi bar
30b3(rgyud): 'gyur ro// nyin gcig bzhin du nang par langs nas tshig tu 'don na/ thos pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// gnod sbyin dang / srin po dang / mkha' 'gro ma thams cad kyi bdang
30b4(rgyud): 'phrog par mi 'gyur zhing / thag ring por yongs su spong bar mi 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de dag dang /
30b5(rgyud): lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// 'phags pa chog/
30b6(rgyud): kyi bdag po'i snying po'i gzungs rdzogs so// // rgya gar skad du/ ar+ya shri dzam b+ha la na ma d+ha ra ne/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa dpal gnod 'dzin zhes
30b7(rgyud): bya ba'i gzungs/ dpal gnod 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das dpal phyag na rdo rje'i pho brang lcang lo tsa
30b8(rgyud): gyis gnas dam pa na/ 'khor gnod sbyin du mas bskor te bzhugs so// de'i tshe gnod sbyin gyi bdag po dpal gnod 'dzin la/ gsang ba'i bdag pos bka' stsal pa/
31a1(rgyud): sems can dbul zhing sdug bsngal ba de dag gi sdug bsngal zhi ba'i phyir/ rang gi srog snying po dang / rig sngags khyod kyis

31a3(rgyud): rig sngags kyis ni bstan par bgyi/ sdug bsngal spong zhing bde ba thob/ tshogs chen gnyis ni rdzogs 'dod pas/ rang lus srung zhing rig sngags 'di/ bzlas zhing
31a4(rgyud): yongs su bzung bar ba// na maHAr+ya dzam b+ha la/ ma hA dzam b+ha la/ tad+ya thA/ ra ra ra ra/ ku nu ku nu/ khu nu khwa nu/ gu nu gu nu/ sa be sa pa/ ka ra ka ra/

31b1(rgyud): bdun chang bar bzlas te/ de'i 'og tu gsang ba'i bdag po'i snying po 'don par 'gyur ro// de yang sngar 'phags pa dkon mchog gsum dang / gsang ba'i bdag po lag
31b2(rgyud): na rdo rje la mchod nas/ de'i 'og tu bdag gis ming nas brjod par bgyid na/ nor rdzas dang ci 'dod pa dag 'grub par bgyid cing bde ba btsal bar bgyid do// de nas bdag
31b3(rgyud): gi gsang sngags yid bzhin nor bu 'di 'don cing yid dam du bgyid na/ de'i dgos pa ci smos pa thams cad sgrubs par bgyid lags so// de nas gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po gnod
31b4(rgyud): 'dzin dpal gyis/ rang nyid kyi snang pa yid bzhin nor bu lta bu dpal phyag na rdo rje la bral ba/ na mo ar+yangs b+ha la/ maspangs b+ha la/ tad+ya ba/ sem sa me/ sus sa ma/

31b7(rgyud): oM dzam b+ha la ma ni b+ha tra ya swA hA/ oM dza ma ba la pra rna b+ha tra ya swA hA/ oM b+ha la na da ya ha tra ya swA hA/ oM dzam b+ha la ma ha d+ha na da b+ha tra ya swA hA/ oM dzam b+ha la tsi pa
31b8(rgyud): kun Da li swA hA/ oM dzam b+ha la ki li mi li/ swA hA/ oM dza ma b+ha la mu khen tra ye swA hA/ oM dza ma b+ha la tsar+yan tra ye swA hA/ de nas gsang ba'i bdag
32a1(rgyud): pos bka' stsal pa/ nor gyis bdag pos khyod kyi gzungs 'di gang gis 'dzin pa dang / 'chang ba dang / 'bri ba dang /

32b1(rgyud): gnod srin mo 'am//

32b8(rgyud): las stong mdzad pa can/ bcom ldan 'das ma grub pa'i a gu li/ Ta ta thA ga ta bi ga ta/ klu mo'i tshigs sum bcus mchod ma/ dza ya dza ya sing d+he/ rgyal
32b9(rgyud): bar mdzad ma/ mi'i mgo thod kyis 'phreng ba can/ hAM kA/ skad cig thang cig yud tsam nyin par gyi bar du dug sel bar/ a su ra de'i da dang / sbyin byed ma'i

33a3(rgyud): drag shul can mo sbrul gyis thos na sbrul 'chi ba'i phyir ro// oM kai li ki li/ ma hA ki li/ ka la rA pi ni/ bgegs thams cad bzlog shig/ pha rol pham par
33a4(rgyud): mdzod ceg/ swA hA/ klags pas grub pa ang gu li snying po dang bcas pa'o// tad+ya thA/ oM d+hu ni d+h+ye ni/ sat+ya t+ye/ a r+yA ha sa/ ni/ d+hu d+ha ne/ ban d+ha ban d+ha/

33b1(rgyud): la sogs pa yo byad thams cad la sngags 'di lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas par bya'o// oM na mo b+ha ga wa te bai ro tsa na pra b+ha rA dza yA/ ta thA ga ta ya/ a ra ha te sa myag
33b2(rgyud): sa bud+ha ya/ tad+ya thA/ oM su k+Sha me su kA me/ sa me sa ma ye/ shan te/ dan te/ a sa ma ro pe/ a na lam b+he/ ta ra ma b+he/ ya sho ba te/ ma hA te dza/ ni ra

33b4(rgyud): gdab pa'i sngags ni/ na ma swa man ta bud+d+hA naM/ oM badz+ra a yu she swA hra/ 'bi 'bi bya ba'i sngags la/ oM badz+ra ud b+ha wa swA hA/ ce te phor bu'i nang du bzhugs

33b6(rgyud): 'bi bi gzhugs pa'i sngags la/ oM badz+ra d+ha tu/ garbe swA hA/ tho bas bsdig cing bsdad pa'i sngags la/ oM badz+ra mud ga ra a ko tra ya hUM phaT swa hA/
33b7(rgyud): ce te'i pur bu nas phyir 'byung ba'i sngags la/ oM badz+ra d+harma ra te swA hA/ 'khor lo dang gdugs gsol ba'i sngags la/ oM badz+ra b+h+ra me na yo swA hA/ tsai te'o

34a1(rgyud): cad du skye ba dran par 'gyur ro// dkyil 'khor byas pa'i lag pa 'jim pa can gyis gang na bar bskus nas/ nad thams cad dang /

44b6(rgyud): te sdig pa smras na/ sdig pa'i 'khor lo rtag tu 'khor de ngan song du lhung ngo // rigs kyi bu de bas na dge ba dang mi dge ba'i yid mi ches su mi rung ngo //
44b7(rgyud): gzhan yang thogs pa med pa/ lus dang sems ni sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi snod yin/ theg pa chen po'i mdo sde bcu gnyis kyis yin te/ thog ma med
44b8(rgyud): pa nas bklags kyang zad mi shes te/ spu'i nyid ma tsam yang ma god do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po mdo sde ni/ rnam par shes pa gcig gis
45a1(rgyud): sems yin te/ rang bzhin mthong ba dag gis ni shes par nus kyis/ tshig du brjod pa 'am/
45a2(rgyud): nyan thos sam/ ma rabs rnams kyis shes par nus pa ni ma yin no// rigs kyi bu gang gis mdo sde 'di bklags te/ don rtog pa dag ni/ lus dang sems
45a3(rgyud): sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi gnod yin par rtogs so// gang bdag gis sems sangs rgyas kyis chos kyis dngos po yin par ma rtogs te/ de la ma mos zhing
45a4(rgyud): blang na rgyun kun 'khor zhing ngan song du ltung ngo // rigs kyi bu de bas na/ dge ba dang mi dge ba la yid mi ches su mi rung ngo // gzhan sdug bsngal gyi rgya mtshor
45a5(rgyud): byings te/ sangs rgyas kyis chos kyi mtshan tsam yang mi thos so/ byang chub sems dpa' thogs pa med pas/ sangs rgyas la yang gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das
45a6(rgyud): 'jig rten na gnas pa'i mi dag ni/ skye ba dang / 'chi ba dang / las lci bar 'dzin pas/ skye ba'i tshe na yang nyi ma ma gdams te dus la babs pa dang skye'o//
45a7(rgyud): shi na yang nyi ma ma gdams ste/ dus la babs pa na shi ba'i slad du'o// shing bgyid pa 'ba' zhig nyi ma bzlas po dang sbyar shing bgyid pa'i 'og tu yang gnod
45a8(rgyud): par 'gyur ba dang / dbul 'phongs pa yang mang la/ rabs chad pa yang nyung ngo / bcom ldan 'das log par lta ba'i sems can dag ni/ ci'i slad du
45b1(rgyud): de ltar gyur pa ma 'tshal te/ de yang dag pa'i lta ba la bgod cing phyin ci log pa gsal du gsol/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ thogs pa med
45b2(rgyud): pa dge'o dge'o// rigs kyi bu khyod kyis sems can skye ba dang / shi ba dang / shing byed pa'i phyir dris pa legs so legs so// khyod kyis legs par nyon
45b3(rgyud): gcig dang / khyod la bstan par bya'o// shes rab kyi tshul dang lam chen po chos gnams langs pas rtag tu sde nyi zla yangs pas rtag tu gsal te/ lo

45b5(rgyud): la bu cig pa dang 'dra bar snying brtse bas/ mi'i dbang por gyur te/ pha ma lta bur gyur pas skye bo'i chos skor gyi yi ge legs dgur bya ba byas nas/ thams
45b6(rgyud): cad kyis dus dang zla tshigs shes par bya ste/ nyi ma mnyam pa dang / gang ba dang / grub pa dang / sdud pa dang / dbang ba dang / gsal ba dang /

45b8(rgyud): pa las thar pa med do// gzhan yang bon pos bcad pa dang / mnan pa dang / bsad par bya zhes tha snyad smras nas/ 'dre gdon la gsol ba 'debs
46a1(rgyud): pa ni/ bdag la gnod pa dang nyon mongs pa'i kha lo byed par zad de/ 'di lta bu gnam gyis dus tshod dang /
46a2(rgyud): sa'i gzhung lugs las 'gal zhing nyi zla'i 'od las brgyab kyis phyogs pa yin te/ rtag tu mun khung du 'thoms nas/ yang dag pa'i lam bde zhing yangs pa
46a3(rgyud): las logs nas/ log pa'i lam du song ba'i ha cang yang phyin ci log ches so// rigs kyi bu gang gis tshe bu btsas pa'i tshe/ mdo sde 'di lan gsum bklags

46a6(rgyud): bzang / zla ba yang rtag tu bzang / lo yang rtag tu bzang bas/ nam yo byad 'byor pa na shing gtong ngo // shing btang ba'i tshe mdo sde 'di lan gsum
46a7(rgyud): bklags na bkra shis chen por 'gyur te/ bsod nams tshad pa thob cing rigs che zhing bcan pa dang / tshe ring ba dang / shi nas kyang 'phags pa'i lam thob par
46a8(rgyud): 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu dur btab pa yang shar lho nub byang gang yang rung te/ gar bde bar ma'i gnas yid du 'ong zhing dga' ba de la 'dre gdon yang der dga'
46b1(rgyud): bar 'gyur te/ mdo sde 'di lan gsum bklags te ngur btab na nam du yang nyes pa mi 'byung zhing / phyug pa dang / me phan pa dang / bkra shis chen por 'gyur
46b2(rgyud): ro ta de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis don de dag bzlas nas tshigs su bcad pa 'di gsungs so// skye ba'i nyi ma bzang la dge// 'chi ba'i dus kyang bzang ba ste// /
46b3(rgyud): skye 'chi'i dus su 'di klags na// phan pa chen po thob par 'gyur// zla ba rtag tu bzang zhing gsal// lo yang rtag tu rab tu bzang // mdo sde bklags te shing
46b4(rgyud): byed na// gzhan du legs shing dge bar 'gyur/ de'i tshe 'khor de na mi bdun khri snyed kyi gsungs pa thos nas sems rnam par grol te/ log pa spangs nas/
46b5(rgyud): yang dag pa la spyod zhing sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi skal pa thob te/ the tshom zad nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob po// de nas byang chub sems
46b6(rgyud): dpa' thogs pa med pas sangs rgyas la gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ma rabs thams cad ni phan tshun yol bar dus bzhi dang / zla tshigs brgyad kyang mngon
46b7(rgyud): par gsal lo// chu dang mi brgyud pa las thams cad gsal lo// pho mo phrad pas bu tsha skyes te/ 'di yang gnam sa'i gzhu lugs kyi tshul yin te/
46b8(rgyud): de ltar 'jug pa ni 'jig rten pa'i chos so// rigs kyi bu glen pa shes rab med pa ni bon lo yid ches te/ bkra shis su re bas mo 'debs kyis/ dge ba
47a1(rgyud): mi byed pas sdig pa rnam pa sna tshogs byas pa'i rkyen gyis/ shi nas phyir yang mi lus thob pa ni sen me'i steng du
47a2(rgyud): chags pa'i rdul dang 'dra'o// sems can dmyal bar ltung ba ni mang / yi dgas dang / byol song du skye ba ni sa chen po dang 'dra'o// rigs kyi bu gal te
47a3(rgyud): gnyen zhig byed na chu dang me ste sngar gcig la gcig 'phrod dam/ mi 'phrod ma ltas par dbang thang che rabs brtsi ba'i yi ge bsdus na dbang thang tshe chub mngon te/
47a4(rgyud): gnyen du 'gyur yang mngon no// bag ma len pa'i nyin par mdo sde 'di lan gsum bklags nas chung ma blangs na/ 'di ni legs pa'i steng du legs pa yin no//
47a5(rgyud): snang ba'i steng du gsal bas mnan pas rigs che ba dang / btsan phyug pa dang / bu cha phan pa dang / yid gzhungs pa dang / shes rab sngo ba dang / shes pa dang ldan
47a6(rgyud): zhing sgra rtsal che ba dang / sri zhu che bar 'gyur te/ shin tu bkre shis pas blo bur du mi 'chi zhing bsod nams dang ldan pa dang / sangs rgyas su 'grub po// de'i tshe
47a7(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' brgyad sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyi rtag tu mi'i nang du gnas te/ thams cad dang mthun par spyod kyang log pa ni bcom/ yang dag pa'i
47a8(rgyud): gzhungs ni 'jugs/ 'dod pa'i yon tan bzhi las rgal te rnam par grol ba brgyad thob pa'i ming la 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' ta ho zag pa zad pa ha/
47b1(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' len kar zag pa zad pa hA/ byang chub sems dpa' ko'u bad to zag pa zad pa hA/ byang chub sems dpa' su bI na shin zag pa zad pa hA/
47b2(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' na la ya na zag pa zad pa hA/ byang chub sems dpa' en rang zag pa zad pa hA/ byang chub sems dpa' dmigs rtog med pa zag pa zad
47b3(rgyud): pa hA/ byang chub sems dpa' ci la yang chags/ pa med pa zag pa zad pa hA/ byang chub sems dpa' 'di brgyad kyis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to//
47b4(rgyud): bdag cag gi sangs rgyas mang po las gzungs su gzungs pa'i rig sngags 'dis/ gang snang brgyad kyi mdo sde 'di 'chang ngam 'dzin pa la/ klog pa dang 'don
47b5(rgyud): pa la nyen pa dang 'jigs pa nam du yang mi 'byung zhing / mi dge ba thams cad kyi gnod pa bsrung zhing bskyab pa'i slad du/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar rig sngags

47b7(rgyud): smra ba log par byed pas 'ongs na/ rig sngags 'di thos pa tsam gyis mgo bo tshal pa bdun du 'gas so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' lus mtha' med pas
47b8(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das ci'i slad du snang brgyad kyi mdo zhes bgyi/ bcom ldan 'das kyis 'khor mang po la phye zhing
48a1(rgyud): bstan te rtogs shing khong du chud pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi mkhyen cing gzigs pa la the tshom yongs su bcad du gsol/

48a6(rgyud): dri rnam par shes pa/ lces ni ro rnam par shes pa/ lus kyi ni rig bya'i rnam par shes pa/ yid kyis ni bye brag 'byed pa'i rnam par shes pa ste/ kun bzhi'i
48a7(rgyud): rnam par shes pa dang / yid kyi rnam par shes pa dang brgyad do// rnam par shes pa brgyad kyi rtsa ba stong zhing ci yang med par rtogs na/ mig gnyis 'od snang ba'i
48a8(rgyud): gnam yin par shes te/ 'od snang ba'i gnam du de bzhin gshegs pas bstan to// kun gzhi'i rnam par shes pa'i gnas las ni/ mdo sde ang ga mang ga
48b1(rgyud): dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i mdo sde chen po byung ngo // yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i gnas las ni/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa 'grel pa'i mdo sde dang / rnal 'byor

48b4(rgyud): gyi thal le bar mtha' med par snang bar byas nas/ mun nag thams cad kyang 'od zer gyis snang bar byas/ sems can dmyal ba thams cad kyang sdug bsngal zhi zhing
48b5(rgyud): thar nas/ bla na med pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed par 'gyur to// de'i tshe 'khor de na byang chub sems dpa' brgyad khri bzhi stong snyed dus gcig tu sangs rgyas su
48b6(rgyud): grub nas/ nyi zla'i 'od zer bya ba'i sangs rgyas su lung ston to// rna ba gnyis ni sgra thos pa'i gnam yin te/ sgra thos pa'i gnam du tshad med pa de bzhin gshegs
48b7(rgyud): pas ston to// sna gnyis sangs rgyas kyi spos kyi gnam yin te/ sangs rgyas kyi spos kyi gnam du/ spos brtsegs pa de bzhin gshegs par ston to// kha dang /
48b8(rgyud): lce ni chos kyi ro'i snod yin te/ chos kyi ro'i snod du chos kyi ro'i de bzhin gshegs par ston to// lus ni rnam par snang mdzad kyi snod yin te/ rnam par snang
49a1(rgyud): mdzad lhun gyi grub pa'i sangs rgyas dang / rnam par snang mdzad 'od zer gyi sangs rgyas dang / rnam par snang mdzad

49b7(rgyud): du thal te/ mdung dang shag tis lus la btsags pa dang / kha nas lcags khu blugs pa dang / rtsa dang rus pa yang zhig snyam pa dang / nyin zhag re la lan
49b8(rgyud): bdun khrin 'chi/ lan bdun khri ni 'tsho ste/ sdug bsngal chen po rgyun sa chad pa 'byung // de yang mdo sde 'di la skur pa btab pa'i phyir 'di 'dra ba zhig spong // de nas bco ldan
50a1(rgyud): 'das kyi sdig pa de dag la tshigs su bcad de bka' stsal pa/ lus ni ye nas yod pa'i lus// yan lag

50b7(rgyud): bzhugs spyod pa de dag thams cad dang / lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / na mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lho 'phye

51a8(rgyud): 'khod do// yang de'i tshe 'khor mang po de na/ bram ze chen po khyab 'jug byin zhes bya ba/ grong khyer dmar bu can na gnas pa/ phyug pa nor mang ba/

52b6(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de ga la bzhugs zhes dris pa dang / yul lnga len na bzhugs so zhes smras pa dang / de nas skye bo'i tshogs de dag 'di snyam du thabs ci zhig bya/
52b7(rgyud): zhes smras pa dang / mi rgan po de na re/ kye me rnams deng la phyogs gtsang mar 'jim pa dang ba lang gi lci bas dkyil 'khor bris la/ sgo bzhi shin tu rnam par phye

53b1(rgyud): pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das/ 'od rab tu mdzes pa'i tog la phyag 'tshal lo phyag 'tshal lo// thub pa sems

185a3(rgyud): swA hA/ ral gri'i snying po'o// ba ru na ta ma a d+hi pa ta ye swA hA/ zhag pa'i snying po'o// pra ban dza na ya swA hA/ rgyal mtshan gyi snying po'o// ma hA su
185a4(rgyud): mya ras ma ye swA hA/ 'khor lo'i snying po'o// b+ha le se bu ye swA hA/ rtse gsum pa'i snying po'o// b+hi la sha hU le swA hA/ phyogs kyi sngags so// sha re
185a5(rgyud): d+ha ya swA hA/ mda'i dra ba'i sngags so// oM ur d+ha dz+wA la badz+ra baun dza ya sA hA/ rdo rje dra ba'i sngags so// 'di rnams dang rang rang gi mkhas pas bum
